  283. I bought this Conair facial sauna (MDF2R)about a month ago and so far i have used it 4 times without any problems. The item is really easy to use out of the box. Before buying this product i was concerned about the safety issue since someone had posted that the blue neck is not long enough and it might be too close to the hot water. Let me clear your doubts, the water is never boiling (bubbling) so there is no splashing going on and there is more then enough room (safety space) between your face and the hot water. You will have to move your face to either sides if you wish to steam those areas. The steam is pretty stationary and only moves while you exhale from your nose. So there is a little learning curve and you will leaned to move your face to the right angle in order to make the steam hit those spots. The easiest way to use the product is on a waist level table OR on a bathroom sink counter while sitting on a chair. That way you will be comfortable and you can hold the base of the steamer with one hand (for safety) and use the other if you wish to keep a towel over your head. So far i have not witnessed any hissing noises since i only use the machine for 15mins or under with still little water left in the reservoir. The timer works pretty good also and it can be turned on only after the water has reached its temperature. I have not used any of the attachments since I don't have any need for them and therefore i will not review on it. I definitely recommend this product if you are in the market for a facial sauna. When i purchased this item little more then a month ago it was 20 bucks even and i see that it has gone down a bit since then so good luck.

While they enjoyed it, it ended up being one of those items that gets infrequent use. I started using it after that. After doing some testing on it myself, I found that there were some good things about it and some that could be improved.<br /><br />PROS:<br />+ Very fair list price and a good value for the mix of functions<br />+ Seems to work relatively well, depending on your needs<br />+ Nice compact size<br />+ Simple controls are intuitive to figure out<br />+ Decent amount of steam is produced quickly<br />+ Timer feature and auto-shut-off will be a pluses for some<br />+ Extra sinus attachment may be useful for some<br />+ Both the normal steamer or sinus attachment help to relieve congestion<br />+ 2 year warrantee is quite generous given the price<br /><br />CONS:<br />- The face brush doesn't produce enough friction to really perform deep cleaning<br />- More heads on the brush would have also been nice<br />- The unit little water, requiring most people to refill it to finish a session<br />- Difficult to position yourself for comfort and full coverage<br />- The edges of the bowl could have been better designed for comfort<br /><br />I am not sure if larger units that hold more water for steaming are sold here. Yet newer versions of the brush concept may not necessarily be better than a washcloth to gently clean away dead layers and dirt from your face.<br /><br />This item works, but there are alternatives. The jury is still out on similar tools, even those with wider cleaning heads like the [[ASIN:B000V2J3ZK Neutrogena Wave Deep Clean Foaming Pad]]. Even tools like the [[ASIN:B0018S8MZ8 Clean & Clear Blackhead Eraser Kit]] may deserve consideration for cleaning out problem areas. More established tools like the [[ASIN:B001884QDK Clarisonic PRO Professional Skin Care System]] have prohibitively high price tags.<br /><br />Many will find that the steam helps not only with skin care but also with opening the sinuses. Higher end steamers are also hard to find, but if you are primarily looking for something to aid your sinuses the [[ASIN:B0000TN7MY Vicks Personal Steam Inhaler]] is probably worth looking into. Finally, the number of creams and other cleansers that may achieve similar results without steaming is almost infinite.<br /><br />If you need steam at the cheapest price, this unit is a good consideration.
